(netwerk/protocol/http/)**\\nFile: netwerk/protocol/http/nsHttpConnection.h and nsHttpConnection.cpp\\nClass: nsHttpConnection\\nDescription: The primary HTTP connection class in Firefox's Necko networking layer. This class manages HTTPS connections by creating and managing the underlying socket transport. When handling HTTPS requests, nsHttpConnection initiates TLS setup through TlsHandshaker.\\n\\n**Hop 2: TLS Handshake Coordinator (netwerk/protocol/http/)**\\nFile: netwerk/protocol/http/TlsHandshaker.h and TlsHandshaker.cpp\\nClass: TlsHandshaker\\nDescription: Responsible for orchestrating the TLS handshake process. It receives callbacks from nsHttpConnection and coordinates SSL initialization via InitSSLParams() and SetupSSL() methods. Acts as a bridge between the HTTP connection layer and SSL socket setup.\\n\\n**Hop 3: Secondary TLS Transport Layer (netwerk/protocol/http/)**\\nFile: netwerk/protocol/http/TLSTransportLayer.h and TLSTransportLayer.cpp\\nClass: TLSTransportLayer\\nDescription: A secondary TLS layer added between nsHttpConnection and the underlying nsSocketTransport. It implements nsISocketTransport interface and wraps input/output streams, providing an additional TLS encryption layer above the socket. It uses PRFileDesc methods to interface with NSS.\\n\\n**Hop 4: SSL I/O Layer Helpers Bridge (security/manager/ssl/)**\\nFile: security/manager/ssl/nsNSSIOLayer.h and nsNSSIOLayer.cpp\\nClass: nsSSLIOLayerHelpers\\nDescription: This class bridges Firefox's Necko networking layer to NSS (Network Security Services). It manages SSL I/O layer creation and configuration. Key functions include nsSSLIOLayerNewSocket() and nsSSLIOLayerAddToSocket() which add the SSL layer to socket file descriptors. These functions are called from nsSSLSocketProvider.\\n\\n**Hop 5: SSL Socket Provider (security/manager/ssl/)**\\nFile: security/manager/ssl/nsSSLSocketProvider.h and nsSSLSocketProvider.cpp\\nClass: nsSSLSocketProvider\\nMethods: NewSocket(), AddToSocket()\\nDescription: Implements nsISocketProvider interface. When Necko needs to create an SSL socket, this provider calls nsSSLIOLayerNewSocket() or nsSSLIOLayerAddToSocket() from nsNSSIOLayer.cpp, which attach the NSS SSL layer to the underlying socket.\\n\\n**Hop 6: NSS SSL Security Layer (security/nss/lib/ssl/)**\\nFile: security/nss/lib/ssl/sslsecur.c\\nKey Functions: ssl_Do1stHandshake(), ssl_FinishHandshake(), SSL_ForceHandshake()\\nDescription: Core SSL handshake orchestration in NSS. The ssl_Do1stHandshake() function is the main entry point that drives the TLS handshake state machine. It repeatedly calls the current handshake function pointer (ss->handshake) until the handshake is complete. These functions receive and process TLS handshake messages.\\n\\n**Hop 7: TLS/SSL3 Connection Handler (security/nss/lib/ssl/)**\\nFile: security/nss/lib/ssl/ssl3con.c\\nKey Functions: ssl3_HandshakeFailure(), ssl3_SendCertificate(), ssl3_ComputeMasterSecret(), ssl3_DeriveConnectionKeys()\\nDescription: Implements the actual TLS 1.2 and TLS 1.3 handshake protocol logic. Contains state machine handlers for processing ClientHello, ServerHello, Certificate, Finished messages, and performing key derivation and encryption setup. Also contains tls13con.h handlers for TLS 1.3 specific operations.\\n\\n**Complete Call Flow:**\\n1. nsHttpConnection::Open() initiates an HTTPS connection\\n2. TlsHandshaker::SetupSSL() is called with the connection info\\n3. TlsHandshaker::InitSSLParams() configures SSL parameters via nsITLSSocketControl\\n4. nsSSLSocketProvider::NewSocket() or AddToSocket() is invoked\\n5. nsSSLIOLayerNewSocket()/AddToSocket() in nsNSSIOLayer.cpp adds SSL layer to PRFileDesc\\n6. NSS I/O layer methods forward I/O to ssl_Do1stHandshake() in sslsecur.c\\n7. ssl_Do1stHandshake() drives the state machine through handshake phases\\n8. ssl3con.c handlers process handshake messages and perform cryptographic operations\\n9. Upon completion, ssl_FinishHandshake() is called and the secure connection is ready\\n\\nThe key innovation is that Firefox's TLSTransportLayer provides an additional abstraction that can wrap existing nsSocketTransport objects, allowing HTTPS-over-HTTPS proxying and CONNECT tunnels without breaking the existing socket abstraction.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2921,"cache_read_input_tokens":73605,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2921},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"6a5ca960-4886-484f-b6c8-bbc92e745907","uuid":"651aeeb9-22a5-48f2-93c1-984eeebe01e9"}

handshake callbacks (SetupSSL, InitSSLParams)\n\n3. **netwerk/protocol/http/TLSTransportLayer** — Secondary TLS encryption layer that wraps socket transport\n\n4. **security/manager/ssl/nsNSSIOLayer (nsSSLIOLayerHelpers)** — Bridges Necko to NSS by managing SSL I/O layer creation\n\n5. **security/manager/ssl/nsSSLSocketProvider** — Socket provider that calls nsSSLIOLayerNewSocket/AddToSocket to attach SSL\n\n6. **security/nss/lib/ssl/sslsecur.c (ssl_Do1stHandshake)** — Orchestrates the TLS handshake state machine\n\n7. **security/nss/lib/ssl/ssl3con.c** — Implements actual TLS 1.2/1.3 protocol logic and cryptographic operations\n\n### **Key Files Identified:**\n- HTTP layer: `nsHttpConnection.h/cpp`, `TlsHandshaker.h/cpp`, `TLSTransportLayer.h/cpp`\n- SSL manager: `nsNSSIOLayer.h/cpp`, `nsSSLSocketProvider.h/cpp`\n- NSS crypto: `sslsecur.c`, `ssl3con.c`\n\nThe answer file includes both the chain of symbols and complete file listing with detailed descriptions of
